x=pd.concat(rows, ignore_index=True)\n        store_promos.append(x)\nif store_promos:\n    spromo=pd.concat(store_promos, ignore_index=True)\n    spromo=spromo.groupby(['store_id','date'], rep stats on primary stores\nrep_store=panel.groupby('primary_rep_id').agg(\n    revenue=('revenue','sum'),\n    units=('units_sold','sum'),\n    customer_count=('customer_count','sum'),\n     a=i+1; b=min(n,i+8)\n        post_rev[i]=c_rev[b]-c_rev[a]\n        post_units[i]=c_units[b]-c_units[a]\n        post_cust[i]=c_cust[b]-c_cust[a]\n    out=g[['store_id','date']].copy()\n Pre/post 7-day metrics per store-date\nouts=[]\nfor store_id, g in daily.groupby('store_id', sort=False):\n    rev=g['revenue'].to_numpy(float)\n    units=g['units'].to_numpy(float)\n    cust=g['customer_count'].to_numpy(float)\n    n=len(g)\n    c_rev=np.r_[0.0, rev.cumsum()]\n    c_units=np.r_[0.0, units.cumsum()]\n    c_cust=np.r_[0.0, cust.cumsum()]\n    idx=np.arange(n)\n    pre_a=np.maximum(0, idx-7)\n    pre_b=idx\n    post_a=idx+1\n    post_b=np.minimum(n, idx+8)\n    pre_rev=c_rev[pre_b]-c_rev[pre_a]\n    pre_units=c_units[pre_b]-c_units[pre_a]\n    pre_cust=c_cust[pre_b]-c_cust[pre_a]\n    post_rev=c_rev[post_b]-c_rev[post_a]\n    post_units=c_units[post_b]-c_units[post_a]\n    post_cust=c_cust[post_b]-c_cust[post_a]\n    out=g[['store_id','date']].copy()\n    out['pre_rev_pc']=pre_rev/pre_cust\n    out['post_rev_pc']=post_rev/post_cust\n    out['pre_units_pc']=pre_units/pre_cust\n    out['post_units_pc']=post_units/post_cust\n    outs.append(out)\nroll=pd.concat(outs, ignore_index=True)\nroll['delta_log_rev_pc']=np.log1p(roll['post_rev_pc'])-np.log1p(roll['pre_rev_pc'])\nroll['delta_log_units_pc']=np.log1p(roll['post_units_pc'])-np.log1p(roll['pre_units_pc'])\n\n# Visits, single-visit store-days only\nvis=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['visit_id','store_id','rep_id','visit_start','visit_type','planned_visit','completed_visit']) for f in sorted(base.glob('store_visit_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\nvis['date']=pd.to_datetime(vis['visit_start']).dt.normalize()\nvis=vis[vis['completed_visit']].copy()\nvis['store_day_visits']=vis.groupby(['store_id','date'])['visit_id'].transform('size')\nvis=vis[vis['store_day_visits']==1].copy()\nvis=vis.merge(roll,on=['store_id','date'],how='left')\nvis['month']=vis['date'].dt.month\nvis['dow']=vis['date'].dt.dayofweek\nvis=vis.dropna(subset=['delta_log_rev_pc','delta_log_units_pc'])\nprint('visits used', len(vis))\n\n# Visit-level audit metrics\nshelf=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['visit_id','facings','shelf_width_cm','endcap_display','checkout_display','promo_stand','pos_materials','planogram_compliance']) for f in sorted(base.glob('shelf_audit_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\ncomp=pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f, usecols=['visit_id','competitor_facings','competitor_promotion']) for f in sorted(base.glob('competitor_audit_*.csv'))], ignore_index=True)\naudit=shelf.groupby('visit_id', as_index=False).agg(\n    facings=('facings','mean'),\n    shelf_width=('shelf_width_cm','mean'),\n    endcap=('endcap_display','mean'),\n    checkout=('checkout_display','mean'),\n    promo_stand=('promo_stand','mean'),\n    pos=('pos_materials','mean'),\n    planogram=('planogram_compliance','mean')\n).merge(comp.groupby('visit_id', as_index=False).agg(comp_facings=('competitor_facings','mean'), comp_promo=('competitor_promotion','mean')), on='visit_id', how='left')\nvis=vis.merge(audit,on='visit_id',how='left')\nvis['exec_score_raw']=0\n# Standardize audit components globally then combine; competitor signs reversed\nfor col, sign in [('facings',1),('shelf_width',1),('endcap',1),('checkout',1),('promo_stand',1),('pos',1),('planogram',1),('comp_facings',-1),('comp_promo',-1)]:\n    s=vis[col]\n    z=(s-s.mean())/s.std(ddof=0)\n    vis['exec_score_raw'] += sign*z\nvis['exec_score_raw'] /= 9\n\n# Absorb fixed effects by iterative demeaning\nfe_cols=['store_id','visit_type','month','dow']\n\ndef absorb(df, ycol, fe_cols, n_iter=30):\n    r=df[ycol].astype(float).to_numpy().copy()\n    grand=np.nanmean(r)\n    r=r-grand\n    # iterative demeaning for multiple FE\n    ser_index=df.index\n    r_ser=pd.Series(r, index=ser_index)\n    for _ in range(n_iter):\n        prev=r_ser.to_numpy().copy()\n        for col in fe_cols:\n            means=r_ser.groupby(df[col]).transform('mean')\n            r_ser = r_ser - means\n        if np.max(np.abs(r_ser.to_numpy()-prev)) < 1e-10:\n            break\n    return r_ser.to_numpy()\n\nresults={}\nfor outcome in ['delta_log_rev_pc','delta_log_units_pc','exec_score_raw']:\n    resid=absorb(vis, outcome, fe_cols)\n    tmp=vis[['rep_id']].copy()\n    tmp['resid']=resid\n    grp=tmp.groupby('rep_id').agg(mean_resid=('resid','mean'), sd=('resid','std'), n=('resid','size'))\n    grp['se']=grp['sd']/np.sqrt(grp['n'])\n    grp['t']=grp['mean_resid']/grp['se']\n    grp['p']=st.t.cdf(grp['t'], df=grp['n']-1)\n    grp['p_adj']=multipletests(grp['p'], method='fdr_bh')[1]\n    results[outcome]=grp\n    print('\\\\nOUTCOME', outcome)\n    print(grp.sort_values('mean_resid').head(20).to_string())\n    sig=grp[(grp['mean_resid']<0)&(grp['p_adj']<0.05)].sort_values('mean_resid')\n    print('sig neg', sig.index.tolist())\n\n# intersection and union summary\nall_ids=sorted(set().union(*[set(df[(df['mean_resid']<0)&(df['p_adj']<0.05)].index.tolist()) for df in results.values()]))\ninter_ids=sorted(set.intersection(*[set(df[(df['mean_resid']<0)&(df['p_adj']<0.05)].index.tolist()) for df in results.values()]))\nprint('\\\\nunion', all_ids)\nprint('intersection', inter_ids)\n\n# combined z score across outcomes (sales revenue, units, exec)\ncombo=pd.DataFrame(index=results['delta_log_rev_pc'].index)\nfor outcome, direction in [('delta_log_rev_pc',1),('delta_log_units_pc',1),('exec_score_raw',1)]:\n    g=results[outcome]\n    combo[outcome+'_z']= (g['mean_resid']-g['mean_resid'].mean())/g['mean_resid'].std(ddof=0)\ncombo['combo']=combo.mean(axis=1)\nprint('\\\\nWorst combo')\nprint(combo.sort_values('combo').head(25).to_string())\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

cust=g['customer_count'].to_numpy(float)\n    n=len(g)\n    c_rev=np.r_[0.0, rev.cumsum()]\n    c_units=np.r_[0.0, units.cumsum()]\n    c_cust=np.r_[0.0, cust.cumsum()]\n    idx=np.arange(n)\n ascending=[True,False,True]).drop_duplicates('store_id')[['store_id','rep_id']].rename(columns={'rep_id':'primary_rep_id'})\n\nstores=pd.read_csv(base/'store_001.csv', usecols=['store_id','store_type','region','location','store_size_sqm'])\nreps=pd.read_csv(base/'sales_rep_001.csv', usecols=['rep_id','region'])\nsp=stores.merge(primary,on='store_id').merge(reps,left_on='primary_rep_id', right_on='rep_id', suffixes=('','_rep'))\nassert (sp['region']==sp['region_rep']).all()\nsp=sp.drop(columns=['rep_id','region_rep'])\n\n# 2) Incremental store-level yearly metrics\nsales_frames=[]\ntraffic_frames=[]\ninv_frames=[]\norder_frames=[]\nfor i in range(1,13):\n    tag=f'{i:03d}'\n    sdf=pd.read_csv(base/f'sales_transaction_{tag}.csv', usecols=['store_id','units_sold','revenue','promo_price'])\n    sdf['promo_units']=np.where(sdf['promo_price']>0, sdf['units_sold'], 0)\n    sales_frames.append(sdf.groupby('store_id').agg(units=('units_sold','sum'), revenue=('revenue','sum'), promo_units=('promo_units','sum')))\n    tdf=pd.read_csv(base/f'store_traffic_{tag}.csv', usecols=['store_id','customer_count'])\n    traffic_frames.append(tdf.groupby('store_id').agg(customer_count=('customer_count','sum')))\n    idf=pd.read_csv(base/f'inventory_status_{tag}.csv', usecols=['store_id','out_of_stock'])\n    inv_frames.append(idf.groupby('store_id').agg(oos_rate=('out_of_stock','mean')))\n    odf=pd.read_csv(base/f'store_order_{tag}.csv', usecols=['store_id','ordered_units'])\n    order_frames.append(odf.groupby('store_id').agg(ordered_units=('ordered_units','sum')))\n\nstore_sales=pd.concat(sales_frames, axis=1).fillna(0).T.groupby(level=0).sum().T.reset_index()\nstore_traffic=pd.concat(traffic_frames, axis=1).fillna(0).T.groupby(level=0).sum().T.reset_index()\nstore_inv=pd.concat(inv_frames, axis=1).fillna(0).T.groupby(level=0).mean().T.reset_index()\nstore_orders=pd.concat(order_frames, axis=1).fillna(0).T.groupby(level=0).sum().T.reset_index()\n\nstore_df=sp.merge(store_sales,on='store_id').merge(store_traffic,on='store_id').merge(store_inv,on='store_id').merge(store_orders,on='store_id')\nstore_df['rev_per_customer']=store_df['revenue']/store_df['customer_count']\nstore_df['units_per_customer']=store_df['units']/store_df['customer_count']\nstore_df['promo_share']=store_df['promo_units']/store_df['units']\nstore_df['orders_per_unit']=store_df['ordered_units']/store_df['units']\n\n# 3) Rep-level store metrics\nrep_store=store_df.groupby('primary_rep_id').agg(\n    revenue=('revenue','sum'),\n    units=('units','sum'),\n    customer_count=('customer_count','sum'),\n    rev_per_customer=('rev_per_customer','mean'),\n    units_per_customer=('units_per_customer','mean'),\n    oos_rate=('oos_rate','mean'),\n    promo_share=('promo_share','mean'),\n    orders_per_unit=('orders_per_unit','mean'),\n    avg_store_size=('store_size_sqm','mean')\n)\nrep_store=rep_store.merge(reps, left_index=True, right_on='rep_id').set_index('rep_id')\nfor c in ['rev_per_customer','units_per_customer','oos_rate','orders_per_unit']:\n    rep_store[c+'_z_by_region']=rep_store.groupby('region')[c].transform(lambda s:(s-s.mean())/s.std(ddof=0))\n\n# 4) Primary-store visit audit score\nvisit_month_dfs=[]\nfor i in range(1,13):\n    tag=f'{i:03d}'\n    vdf=pd.read_csv(base/f'store_visit_{tag}.csv', usecols=['visit_id','store_id','rep_id'])\n    vdf=vdf.merge(primary,on='store_id',how='left')\n    vdf=vdf[vdf['rep_id']==vdf['primary_rep_id']][['visit_id','rep_id']]\n    sdf=pd.read_csv(base/f'shelf_audit_{tag}.csv', usecols=['visit_id','facings','shelf_width_cm','endcap_display','checkout_display','promo_stand','pos_materials','planogram_compliance'])\n    cdf=pd.read_csv(base/f'competitor_audit_{tag}.csv', usecols=['visit_id','competitor_facings','competitor_promotion'])\n    adf=sdf.groupby('visit_id', as_index=False).agg(\n        facings=('facings','mean'), shelf_width=('shelf_width_cm','mean'), endcap=('endcap_display','mean'),\n        checkout=('checkout_display','mean'), promo_stand=('promo_stand','mean'), pos=('pos_materials','mean'),\n        planogram=('planogram_compliance','mean')\n    )\n    cagg=cdf.groupby('visit_id', as_index=False).agg(comp_facings=('competitor_facings','mean'), comp_promo=('competitor_promotion','mean'))\n    visit_month_dfs.append(vdf.merge(adf,on='visit_id',how='left').merge(cagg,on='visit_id',how='left').dropna())\nvisit_audit=pd.concat(visit_month_dfs, ignore_index=True)\nfor col, sign in [('facings',1),('shelf_width',1),('endcap',1),('checkout',1),('promo_stand',1),('pos',1),('planogram',1),('comp_facings',-1),('comp_promo',-1)]:\n    visit_audit[col+'_z']=sign*(visit_audit[col]-visit_audit[col].mean())/visit_audit[col].std(ddof=0)\nvisit_audit['audit_score']=visit_audit[[c for c in visit_audit.columns if c.endswith('_z')]].mean(axis=1)\nrep_audit=visit_audit.groupby('rep_id').agg(audit_score=('audit_score','mean'), n_visits=('visit_id','size'))\nrep=rep_store.join(rep_audit, how='left')\nrep['audit_score_z_by_region']=rep.groupby('region')['audit_score'].transform(lambda s:(s-s.mean())/s.std(ddof=0))\n\n# 5) Composite: bad sales + bad stock/order + bad audit\nrep['badness'] = (\n    -rep['rev_per_customer_z_by_region']\n    -rep['units_per_customer_z_by_region']\n    +rep['oos_rate_z_by_region']\n    -rep['orders_per_unit_z_by_region']\n    -rep['audit_score_z_by_region']\n)/5\n\nprint('Worst reps by composite badness')\nprint(rep.sort_values('badness', ascending=False)[[\n    'region','badness','rev_per_customer_z_by_region','units_per_customer_z_by_region',\n    'oos_rate_z_by_region','orders_per_unit_z_by_region','audit_score_z_by_region'\n]].head(30).to_string())\n\nprint('\\\\nComposite distribution')\nprint(rep['badness'].describe().to_string())\n\n# Also show reps that are poor across all dimensions (3+ bad z thresholds)\nfor thresh in [1.0,1.25,1.5]:\n    flags=((rep['rev_per_customer_z_by_region']<-thresh).astype(int)\n           +(rep['units_per_customer_z_by_region']<-thresh).astype(int)\n           +(rep['oos_rate_z_by_region']>thresh).astype(int)\n           +(rep['orders_per_unit_z_by_region']<-thresh).astype(int)\n           +(rep['audit_score_z_by_region']<-thresh).astype(int))\n    print(f'\\\\nthreshold {thresh}')\n    print(rep.assign(flag_count=flags).sort_values(['flag_count','badness'], pre_b=idx\n    post_a=idx+1; post_b=np.minimum(n, idx+8)\n    pre_rev=c_rev[pre_b]-c_rev[pre_a]; post_rev=c_rev[post_b]-c_rev[post_a]\n    pre_units=c_units[pre_b]-c_units[pre_a]; post_units=c_units[post_b]-c_units[post_a]\n    pre_cust=c_cust[pre_b]-c_cust[pre_a];
